 The Reserve Bank of India directed banks not to give loans to buy gold in any form
 bank ab primary gold, sarrapha yaa aabhushan sahit kisi bhi rup main sone ko kharidne ke liye rin nahin denge
 The central bank has taken this step to protect people from engaging in any speculative activity
 kendriya bank ne ek adhisuchana main kaha he
 
 
 'it is advised that loans should not be given by the bank to buy gold in any form
 ' The forms of gold mentioned in the notification are primary gold, gold bullion, gold jewelery, gold coin, gold ETF unit and gold mutual fund unit
 haalanki isamen kaha gaya he ki bank johariyon kii uchit kriyasheel puunji jaruraton ke liye dhan de sakate hai
 The comments kendriya bank ne sone ke aayaat main haal hi main ai acchhee khaasi badhotari ko dekhte hue yah kadam uthaaya he
 This led to increasing pressure on the current account deficit
 vittvarsh 2011-12 main bharat kaa sone kaa aayaat 60 arab dollar mulya kaa rahaa jabaki maatra 1,067 ton rahi
 Banks will no longer loan to buy gold in any form, including primary gold, bullion or jewelery
 kendriya bank ne yah kadam logon ko kisi satoria gatividhi main shaamil hone se bachaane ke liye uthaaya he
 The central bank said in a notification
 
 
 'salaah di jaati he ki bank dwaara kisi bhi rup main sona kharidne ke liye rin nahin diya janaa chahie
 ' sone ke jin roopon kaa adhisuchana main ullekh kiya gaya he unamem primary gold, sona sarrapha, sona aabhushan, sona sikaa, sona itief ikai tathaa sona mutual fund ikai he
 However, it states that banks can provide funds for the proper working capital requirements of jewelers
 tippaniyan The central bank has taken this step in view of the recent significant increase in gold imports
 iske chalate chaalu khaataa ghate par dabaav bad rahaa tha
 India's gold imports stood at $ 60 billion in fiscal year 2011-12, while the quantity stood at 1,067 tonnes

 Aaj Tak correspondent Gopi Ghanghar had a special conversation with Gujarat Chief Minister Anandiben Patel
 is dauraan unhone bataaya ki piem modi apane janmdin ke maukey par gujarat main rahenge
 Question- Narendra Modi's central government and your government have completed 100 days
 aap is bare main kya sochati hai?jawaab-deshbhar main modi sarkaar ke liye jo aashaa ore apeksha thi, wo us par khara utarane kaa puri tarah se prayaas kar rahe hai
 On August 15, during a speech from the ramparts of the Red Fort, he had spoken of having bank accounts of people across the country and within 15 days he started the Jan Dhan Yojana
 aisi kai yojanaayen narendrabhai ne shuru kin
 Petrol prices are also coming down, due to which inflation is being curbed
 main jab dekhati hum, gujarat ke bare main hamane lakshya rakhaa tha gatisheel gujarat

 teen maheene main ye kaam puraa karnaa he

 hamane jo points tay kiye the wo puure ho jaaenge
 Question- Is Gujarat now a Modi bin? Answer - No, Gujarat is not a Modi bin

 donon aa rahe hai, mulaakaat hogi emoyu sin hoga itnaa hamen pataa he

 i will not go with them

 What is the validity of the e-way bill? The validity of the e-way bill is fixed
 yah is par nirbhar karegaa ki koi saamaan yaa vastu kitni duuri tak transport kiya janaa he
 If you are sending any goods or goods worth more than Rs
 50 thousand within 100 km or within the normal vehicle and transport medium, then the e-way bill will be valid for one day
 vahiin agar saamaan ower diamensional cargo whical se bheja ja rahaa he, to har 20 kilometre or iske daayre main ja rahe saamaan ke liye janaret hue i-ve bill kii vaidhata bhi ek din hi hogi
 How to calculate validity? Suppose you released the e-way bill on April 14 at 00:04
 aise main pehla din 15-16 april kii madhyaraatri 12:00 baje khatm hoga
 At the same time, the second day of 16-17 will end at 12 noon
 vahiin, agar koi i-ve bill 14 april kii 23
 58 (11 of the night
 58 baje ) janaret kiya gaya he, to pehla din 15-16 april kii madhyaraatri 12 baje tak vaid hoga
 At the same time, the second day will be considered till 12 noon of 16-17 April
 validity ko badha sakate hai kya?i-ve bill kii vaidhata ko badhaayaa ja saktaa he, lekin yah kuch khaas paristhitiyon main hi kiya ja saktaa he
 According to the government, due to natural disaster, law and order, accident and other reasons, the validity can be increased
 haalanki validity badhaane ke dauraan vajah kii puri jaankaree deni jaruri he

 uske baad 1962 main congress ke hi shaam nath ne

 In 1977, the Bali overturned and the seat fell to the BLD

 In 1991, Tarachand Khandelwal won from BJP and reached Parliament
 1996 main congress ke jai prakaash agarwal yahaan se saansad bane
